<Review>The dentists there are incredibly kind and very welcoming. The person that first saw me, (Lino I believe?) was really cool. Dr Shalaby didn't try to scold me like most dentists do and made me feel very comfortable. Also you could tell that he really focuses on preventative care, and doesn't try to do fillings if he doesn't need to. I have an appointment for my fillings tomorrow. The technology is quite advanced and they do a very in depth job of going over the x-rays.

The hygienist was really nice and very warm and friendly like the rest. My only complaint is in terms of a cleaning it was probably the worst one I've ever had. It's not that he does anything wrong and he seems very knowledgeable it's just that it's incredibly short (I think it's just scheduled that way, I don't think it has anything to do with the hygienist at all). My last cleaning at another office (the actual procedure) lasted around 45 minutes. She used the pick for 20 minutes, polished, lasered, etc. It was very in depth and my teeth (although sore) felt amazingly clean. They felt so clean for the next few MONTHS it was that good.

This one the actual cleaning procedure lasted maybe 15 minutes at best, and that's only because of the extra fluoride polishing procedure I had to purchase that wasn't covered by my free cleaning. He used the pick on my front bottom teeth for a few minutes then had a little polisher that really didn't feel like it did much for about another 2-3 minutes. That was it. My teeth felt the same as I had walked in, with a little bit of fluoride paste on them. I almost felt like calling up another dentist and scheduling my second free cleaning (covered by my insurance) on the spot.

Like I said the overall experience was good, and better than most dentist's I've been to because of how personable they are. And the price is very reasonable. Just a suggestion is to be more in depth with the cleaning, as a lot of people are in there just for the cleaning so people should get a better experience out of it. I'm happy to go back there for my fillings, and will update the post with my most likely very positive experience.<//Review>< Pictures>
